\n  \nWe believe there’s a Ramblin’ Man - or Ramblin’ Woman - in all of us who wants to wander and listen to great music, drink fine beer, eat great food and have the best of times. Live life to the full and take it as it comes as you join the Ramblin’ Family from 2015 \n  \nScroll down to the bottom of this page for accommodation packages inc Hotels and offsite camping.  \n  \nQ & A's \n  \nWhen will Ramblin'Man Fair take place?  \nOn Saturday 25th July 2015 and Sunday 26th July 2015. \n What are the opening and closing time for Ramblin'Man Fair? \nSaturday 25th July 2015 midday to 11pm, Sunday 26th July 2015 midday to 10.30pm \n Where will Ramblin'Man Fair take place? \nMote Park, Mote Avenue, Maidstone, Kent, ME15 7SU \n Am I able to leave the site during the day and come back in? \nWeekend VIP Admission, Weekend General Admission and Day VIP Admission ticket holders may leave the site and return provided they have a wristband that is undamaged on their return. Day General Admission ticket holders will not be able to leave the site and return. \n  \nIs there camping at the Festival? \n There is no general camping on the festival site but there are Glamping a the Ranch Accommodation Packages available at Mote Park, as well as Hotel Packages and Offsite Camping Packages all available from the Accommodation section of the Ramblin' Man Fair website - www.ramblinmanfair.com   \n  \nIs there disabled access? \n The site is accessible to disabled customers. Please see our Information page for more detail or contact info@ramblinmanfair.com. \n  \nI am travelling by train, where is the nearest station? \n You have the choice of three local stations: Maidstone West (8 minute walk) Maidstone East (15 minute walk) Maidstone Barracks (18 minute walk). Train services are provided by Southeastern trains and late trains will be provided each day of the Fair. \n  \nIs there parking available at Ramblin'Man Fair? \n There will be no parking available at Mote Park (or in the roads surrounding the park) unless you have purchased a Glamping at the Ranch Accommodation Package. Disabled parking is available for blue badge holders at Mote Park. Park and Rides / Walks will be made available for all ticket purchasers and journey times are anticipated to be less than 10 minutes. Information on the locations and how to book Park and Rides will be made available in early 2015. \n  \nWhat are the benefits of VIP? \n VIP benefits include fast access to the festival through the VIP entrance; access to the exclusive VIP area with luxury toilets, bar/food offerings, and chill out area; priority queuing for return shuttle bus services to Hotels, Off-Site Camping and Park and Rides; readmission for Day ticket holders. \n  \nCan I bring food and drink into the Fair? \n You will not be able to bring alcohol onto the site but can bring a 500ml bottle of water that can be refilled. There will be plenty of bars on site selling a variety of drinks at reasonable prices. You can bring a small amount of precooked food of the snack variety. There will be a large selection of food outlets to cater for all tastes at reasonable prices. \n  \nAre there any age restrictions? \n  \n  \nThere is no age restriction at Ramblin’ Man Fair. Tickets are free to children under the age of 12 years. All attendees under 16 years of age must be accompanied by a parent/guardian (person over 18 years of age). Parents/guardians should purchase their own tickets through the normal channel and bring under 12’s to the entrance on arrival at the Fair to be provided with complimentary access (wristband if required). Please note proof of age may be requested which should be a passport or birth certificate. All children 12 years of age and older will require a full price ticket for the Fair. Children do not require a ticket to access Glamping at the Ranch provided they are accompanied by a parent/guardian that has purchased the accommodation and has a weekend ticket. \nPlease note that parents or guardians are responsible for their child’s safety and welfare at all times. Please take into account that there may be elements of the festival that are not suitable for young children. Ear defenders are strongly recommended for all children as loud music can damage hearing. \n  \nWill there be any seating areas? \n There will be areas to sit down on the site and grandstand seating at the Classic Rock stage will be available to purchase in early 2015. \n  \nCan I bring a deck chair? \n At present you cannot bring a deck chair but we are reviewing this policy with our safety team. \n  \nWhen will my membership to TeamRock+ start and how long will it last? \n All tickets include a membership to TeamRock+. Weekend Tickets include 6 months membership, Day tickets include 3 months membership, and Founders Club includes 12 months membership. The membership will start approximately 14 days after you have purchased your ticket. You will be contacted directly by TeamRock with regard to setting the membership up. \n  \nI can't find an answer to my question, who can I contact? \n For further information please contact:
